<user_name>Sasha<//user_name><Date>1549753741116< /Date><rating>5< /rating>< review>
Best pizza in the Sacramento area, in quality, quantity, and price. Do yourself a favor and check them out. I used to treat myself to Round Table, Mountain Mikes, and BJ's, but they are all way too over priced. That, and the service and quality of food I've received from them has been sub par at best (see my previous reviews). But Original Pizza House? I've been ordering from them now for over four years, and I've not once had a bad experience, bad customer service, or bad food. So yummy! So fresh! I'm in pizza heaven! <3</review>

<text>Been coming here for years now.
Service has been pretty good and orders have come out quick unless they are super busy.

Pizzas have been good. Lots of options and some pretty good gourmet pizzas too. Try the lamb pizza or creat your own masterpiece.

The calzones are also good.

They always have deals from the flyer or just call and ask.

Usually everything is hot and ready in the time frame given whilst placing your order.   It seems that when business is slower (slower than their normal rush for dinner or lunch), when you arrive at the time quoted,  it seems like the pizza may have gotten done a bit early and isn't as hot and fresh as normal.   They have just gotten me used to such excellent quality that when it isn't,  it is very evident. 3< /Rating>
< Text>
Pretty decent park. The kids like the large field and I like that there are clean, well-stocked restrooms on site. There are also several large park benches for picnics, and the playground equipment has a shade cover.

Two disadvantages: there are only baby swings,  (not swings for the big kids) and there are often shady people passing through. The proximity to the freeway make the parking lot a desirable location for people to do suspicious things. Other than that, the park itself is okay.< /Text>

<rate>1</rate>< text>
The only thing shiftier than a rental car is this co-branded Avis/Budget franchisee. Arrived at the 7:30 am opening time to pick up the car I reserved online for $70/weekend. The printed contract stated $130. When asked about the discrepancy the owner said 'it's $60 for the extra 30 minutes beyond three days'.  Huh? By now it's 7:40 am. Turns out the following Monday is a holiday and they don't open until 8 am. Since I "can't return (the car) until 8 am, it's an extra $60 'late fee'".

OK-I'll wait 20 minutes, rent the car today at 8:00 am and thus stay within the three day window. "Too late," he quips, "the transaction is complete and your credit card's been charged!"  When I challenged his lack of a signed rental agreement he countered "all I can do now is void your existing reservation and book a new one" -at a substantially higher price. No thanks. As I walked out he magically gained the ability to credit my previously 'unchangeable' 7:30 am "transaction" $60-but only after I returned the car, and (naturally) with nothing confirmed in writing.

Righhhht.  Read the other reviews for how these shady undocumented future 'promises' have played out. I can only imagine the return damage inspection.

Walked across the street, hopped in a Gig-car, drove where I needed to go and conveniently "returned" it right in front of my own house. No slight-of-contract shenanigans, trumped-up damages or belligerent business owners necessary-and with the fuel included Gig turned out to be cheaper!

UPDATE:  Adding insult to injury, the response from "socialinfo@Avis" was just empty-Google-review-fixing.  Never heard a peep back.  Nice work, Avis.</text>

<text>BEWARE!!!

My biggest complaint is that they charged my first appointment $500!!!!
I found another chiropractor that told me that that fee was ridiculous and they overpriced me for the appointment. They charged me $250 for the examination which consist of Dr. Blum touching my back for a minute. They charged me another $100 for the X-Rays. $125 for the adjustment. They charged me $15 for laying down on a couple cold packs after the adjustment. Then they let me keep the cold pack. They made it seem like the cold pack was going to be for free, but they end up charging me $10 to keep the cold pack.

I left the office feeling like I did not get a proper treatment.

This practice is not upfront about their fees until after they've already provided you the services.

< text>
Pros: Great place to get cheap and affordable groceries. Always check the dates on things. The reason things are cheaper is that items usually do not have a very long expiration date.

Cons: The cashout lines are very long because there are usually only two registers open. If you are looking for the same items on a weekly basis do not bother, not everything is stocked consistently. The checking of IDs for alcoholic beverages is questionable. According to what I've seen is that I have been born in many different years on multiple occasions.

All in all it is a decent place close by in the SJ downtown to grab some affordable groceries without having to break the bank.< /text>

<Name>Brian Hiles< /Name>< review>
A moderately-sized store of a well organized and reasonably comprehensive inventory, comprising food (with a few pre-mixed salads etal), sundries (matts, storage containers, kitchen items, etal), and health items (vitamins, supplements, non-prescription meds, etal).

Low prices are the real selling point! I don't need to go to the local CostCo anymore for select staples.
